Hairy crabs, salmon, and grilled shrimps are all very fresh and unlimited. Each dish is prepared with high quality and tastes good. Special mention should be made to Manager Bao Lei and Director Hou in the buffet restaurant. Their thoughtful and meticulous service throughout the entire process made us feel at home. The room attendants He Li and Wang Nuyan were very considerate and provided disposable items in a timely manner. I have to say that choosing to stay at Furama Hotel was a great experience. It made our trip to Dalian enjoyable and we left no regrets. Thank you so much.
